==============================
FILE: 11.6 Magics/11.6.1 Runes.md
==============================

All runes can be purchased as single use items from stores. They can then be used for enchanting and spells.
# Runic Inscription (Enchanting)
Runes are ancient symbols etched into items to tap into the fundamental forces of the world.
- Xeran Runes: Used for Permanent Enchantments. Once applied, the item is permanently changed.
- Vindroth Runes: Used for Spellcasting. Will be explained lower down.
### Runic Logic & Constraints
- A single Xeran rune can be etched onto an item with no penalty. However, if you wish to place two or more effect runes on a single object, they must be bound within a Runic Circle.
- Enchanted items cannot be modified. You must decide the full runic array before the first inscription.
- A single runic circle can support a maximum of 10 Effect Runes.
- The Carbon Ratio: In any circle, the volatile energies must be balanced by Carbon Runes. The formula is:
	- *Number of Carbon Runes = Number of Effect Runes - 1*
## Inscription Requirements & Circle Scaling
Creating a runic circle requires a base Mana expenditure plus the cost of the individual runes.

|**Effect Runes**|**Carbon Runes**|**Total Circle Size**|**Mana Surcharge**|**Level Req.**|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|**1**|0|1|+0|1|
|**2**|1|3|+5|1|
|**3**|2|5|+10|3|
|**4**|3|7|+20|6|
|**5**|4|9|+80|12|
|**6**|5|11|+600|21|
|**7**|6|13|+1,200|30|
|**8**|7|15|+2,400|40|
|**9**|8|17|+4,800|55|
|**10**|9|19|+9,600|70|
## Xeran Rune Effects Table
Effects stack. If a weapon has two Fire runes, it deals +2d6 Fire damage and so on.

| **Rune**   | **Effect (Weapon)**                     | **Effect (Armor)**                      | **Mana Cost** | DC Mod | Affinity | Cost       |
| ---------- | --------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------- | ------------- | ------ | -------- | ---------- |
| Carbon     | None (Stabilizer)                       | None (Stabilizer)                       | 0             | 0      | Generic  | 1 Gold     |
| Strengthen | +1 Accuracy Bonus                       | +1 Armor Class (AC)                     | 10            | 3      | Generic  | 2 Gold     |
| Unbreaking | Item is indestructible                  | Item is indestructible                  | 100           | 8      | Generic  | 5 Platinum |
| Burst      | On hit: 1d4 Fire + 1d4 Force (10ft AOE) | On hit: 1d4 Fire + 1d4 Force (10ft AOE) | 150           | 6      | Fire     | 5 Gold     |
| Fire       | +1d6 Fire Damage                        | Resist 1d4 Fire damage/hit              | 25            | 4      | Fire     | 3 Gold     |
| Earth      | +1d6 Earth Damage                       | Resist 1d4 Earth damage/hit             | 25            | 4      | Earth    | 3 Gold     |
| Water      | +1d6 Water Damage                       | Resist 1d4 Water damage/hit             | 25            | 4      | Water    | 3 Gold     |
| Air        | +1d6 Air Damage                         | Resist 1d4 Air damage/hit               | 25            | 4      | Air      | 3 Gold     |
| Force      | +1d6 Force Damage                       | Resist 1d4 Physical damage/hit          | 25            | 4      | Generic  | 3 Gold     |
| Necrotic   | +1d6 Necrotic Damage                    | Resist 1d4 Necrotic damage/hit          | 50            | 6      | Necrotic | 1 Platinum |
| Radiant    | +1d6 Radiant Damage                     | Resist 1d4 Radiant damage/hit           | 50            | 6      | Radiant  | 1 Platinum |
| Psychic    | +1d6 Psychic Damage                     | Resist 1d4 Psychic damage/hit           | 75            | 7      | Psychic  | 5 Platinum |
## The Inscription Ritual
Inscribing a runic array is a delicate process of channeling mana through physical matter. To successfully enchant an item, a crafter must perform a sequence of Inscription Checks, one for every rune in the array (including Carbon runes).

1. The Inscription Check
	- For each rune, roll a d20 and add your Relevant Affinity Modifier.
	- The Base DC is 12 and it goes up depending on the DC Mod (see above table).
	- Example: Inscribing a Fire Rune has a total DC of 16.

2. The Ritual Sequence
	- If you are creating a Runic Circle, you must roll for every rune in the circle in one continuous session. 
	- If you pass the roll, the rune is successfully etched. Move to the next rune in the array.
	- Critical Success (Natural 20): The rune is etched perfectly; you gain Advantage on the next roll in the sequence.

3. Failed Inscriptions & Unstable Mana
	- If a single roll in the sequence fails or you are interrupted, the ritual fails and the item becomes Saturated with unstable mana.
	- The item cannot be enchanted further, and the current runes provide no bonuses.
	- To clear the Saturated state, you must spend 1 Hour and 100 Mana to fix the item. Once fixed, the item is restored to its original, non-magical state and can be enchanted again from scratch.
	- All runes that were used are destroyed in the process
# Vindroth Runes
Vindroth runes are written as sentence structures (often called _paragraphs_), allowing rune magic to function like a programmed trigger system, when a condition is met, an effect occurs. Vindroth runes are not arranged in circles. Instead, they are inscribed as ordered “words” that form a readable sequence (ex: If … Than … Else …).
### Inscription Rules
- Each Vindroth rune occupies 1 square inch of space.
- All runes in a paragraph must be inscribed into one continuous piece of material.
- If the material has a complete break that separates words, the paragraph loses the separated words. This may weaken, change, or fully disable the effect.
### Vindroth Structure Limits
A Vindroth paragraph is limited by your Level.
- You may include 1 “If … Than” block per your Level/2.
- Every 2 Levels also increases how many logic-connectors you may include (Else / And / Or / Not).
### Using Xeran as Effect Payloads
Vindroth can call Xeran runes as effect payloads (usually to define damage type / element / output).
Example structure:
- If object (human) entered size (5) shape (sphere) Than Power (Xeran Fire)
To increase output, you may repeat effect runes:
- … Than Power (Xeran Fire) And Power (Xeran Fire)
With each And Power adding another damage as well as consuming 1 Structure Limit
## Vindroth Conditionals

| Rune          | Effect                                                                                                       | Cost     |
| ------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | -------- |
| If            | Begins a conditional check.                                                                                  | 5 Silver |
| Than          | Executes the next statement(s) if the condition is true.                                                     | 5 Silver |
| Else          | Executes the next statement(s) if the previous condition was false (may be followed by **If**).              | 5 Silver |
| And           | Combines conditions/effects; both must apply (when used with **If**) or both occur (when used with effects). | 5 Silver |
| Or            | Combines conditions; either condition being true is sufficient.                                              | 5 Silver |
| Not           | Negates a condition (true only if the condition is not met).                                                 | 5 Silver |
| at            | Specifies the point of origin / location where the effect occurs.                                            | 1 Silver |
| while         | Keeps the effect active as long as the condition remains true.                                               | 1 Silver |
| size          | Defines area size; maximum area is **5 × Vindroth School Level**.                                            | 1 Silver |
| shape         | Defines area shape (sphere, cube, spear (directional attack)).                                               | 1 Silver |
| object        | Defines what is being checked or targeted (leave blank to mean “any”).                                       | 1 Silver |
| within        | True if the object is within the specified range/area.                                                       | 1 Silver |
| entered       | True if the object enters the specified range/area.                                                          | 1 Silver |
| value         | Stores a named value (variable).                                                                             | 1 Silver |
| equals        | True if two values are equal.                                                                                | 1 Silver |
| greater       | True if the first value is greater than the second.                                                          | 1 Silver |
| lesser        | True if the first value is less than the second.                                                             | 1 Silver |
| has           | True if the object has a specified property/flag/mark.                                                       | 1 Silver |
| lacks         | True if the object lacks a specified property/flag/mark.                                                     | 1 Silver |
| self          | True if the object is the caster.                                                                            | 1 Silver |
| touched       | True if the inscribed surface is touched.                                                                    | 1 Silver |
| moved         | True if the object moved.                                                                                    | 1 Silver |
| attacked      | True if the object attacked.                                                                                 | 1 Silver |
| damaged       | True if the object took damage.                                                                              | 1 Silver |
| healed        | True if the object was healed.                                                                               | 1 Silver |
| cast          | True if the object casts a spell.                                                                            | 1 Silver |
| chance        | Roll 1d10 and return the number (usable with comparisons like greater/lesser/equals).                        | 1 Silver |
| direction     | Specifies a direction (up/down/north/south/east/west). You may also use Xeran direction runes for this.      | 1 Silver |
| throw (Type)  | Specifies the saving throw type used by an effect.                                                           | 1 Silver |
| throw (Value) | Specifies the save DC. The DC cannot exceed 10 + Generic Affinity.                                           | 1 Silver |
| delay         | Delays an effect in 6-second intervals, max 18 × Level.                                                      | 1 Silver |
## Vindroth Effects

| Rune            | Effect                                                                                                                       | Cost      |
| --------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------- |
| Power           | Deal 1d4 damage (damage type defined by the attached Xeran element, if any) (counts as a spell attack using generic affinity | 20 Silver |
| Heal (Vitality) | Heal 1d6 Vitality.                                                                                                           | 20 Silver |
| Heal (Health)   | Heal 1d4 Hit Points.                                                                                                         | 40 Silver |
| Create          | Create a specified Xeran element.                                                                                            | 80 Silver |
| Resist          | Grant resistance to a specified damage type.                                                                                 | 20 Silver |
| Vulnerable      | Grant vulnerability to a specified damage type.                                                                              | 20 Silver |
| Dispel          | Counterspell all castings in range with mana cost lower than 20 × Mana imbued into rune during inscription.                  | 20 Silver |
| Add             | Add a specified number to a specified value (number is defined by mana put into the rune during inscription).                | 20 Silver |
| Subtract        | Subtract a specified number from a specified value (number is defined by mana put into the rune during inscription).         | 20 Silver |
| Multiply        | Multiply a specified value by a specified number (number is defined by mana put into the rune during inscription).           | 20 Silver |
| Divide          | Divide a specified value by a specified number (number is defined by mana put into the rune during inscription).             | 20 Silver |
| Mark            | Apply a named mark to a target. The mark is invisible, but can be detected by has rune.                                      | 20 Silver |
| Push            | Move the target in the specified direction (Strength save 10 + Generic Affinity).                                            | 20 Silver |
| Trap            | Apply the Prone condition (Strength save 10 + Generic Affinity).                                                             | 20 Silver |
## Example Castings

### Simple Fire Trap (Entry Trigger)
**Structure**
```
If object (any) entered size (5) shape (sphere)
Than Power (Xeran Fire)
```
**What it Does**  
Deals 1d4 Fire damage to any creature that enters a 5 ft sphere around the inscription.

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1
- Logic connectors: 0

**Minimum Level**
- **1**

**Notes**  
Baseline Vindroth usage. This is the canonical rune trap example.
### Healing Plate (Touch Trigger)
**Structure**
```
If object (self) touched
Than Heal
```
**What it Does**  
When the caster touches the inscribed surface, they heal 1d4 HP.

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1
- Logic connectors: 0

**Minimum Level**
- **1**
### Directional Force Push Trap
**Structure**
```
If object (any) entered size (5) shape (sphere)
Than Push direction (north)
```
**What it Does**  
Any creature entering the area must make a Strength save or be pushed north.

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1
- Logic connectors: 0

**Minimum Level**
- **1**
### Conditional Trap with Else Clause
**Structure**
```
If object (self) entered size (5) shape (sphere)
Than Heal (Vitality)
Else Power (Xeran Necrotic)
```
**What it Does**
- If the caster enters: heal 1d6 Vitality
- Otherwise: intruders take 1d4 Necrotic damage

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1
- Else clauses: 1

**Minimum Level**
- **4**
### Mana-Scaling Kill Zone
**Structure**
```
While object (any) within size (10) shape (sphere)
Than Power (Xeran Fire)
And Power (Xeran Fire)
And Power (Xeran Fire)
```
**What it Does**  
Deals 3d4 Fire damage to all creatures within the area each turn until they leave area

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1 (while)
- Logic connectors: 2 (extra Power via And)

**Minimum Level**
- **6**
### Damage with Save and Delay
**Structure**
```
If object (any) entered size (5) shape (sphere)
Than delay (6)
And Power (Xeran Fire)
And throw (Dex)
And throw (10)
```
**What it Does**  
After 6 seconds, deals 1d4 Fire damage to creatures in the area, Dex save (10) to resist.

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 1
- Logic connectors: 3 (delay, And Power, And throw)

**Minimum Level**
- **8**
### Mark-and-Execute Rune
**Structure**
```
If object (any) entered size (5) shape (sphere)
Than Mark (prey)

If object (any) has (prey)
And attacked
Than Power (Xeran Fire)
And Power (Xeran Fire)
```
**What it Does**
- First trigger: entering marks the target.
- Second trigger: if a marked target attacks, they take 2d4 Fire damage.

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 2
- Logic connectors: 2

**Minimum Level**
- **8**
### Smart Defense Engine
**Structure**
```
If object (any) entered size (20) shape (sphere)
And lacks (ally)
Than Mark (hostile)

If object (any) has (hostile)
And cast
Than Dispel

If object (any) has (hostile)
And attacked
Than Power (Xeran Force)
And Power (Xeran Force)
And throw (Str)
And throw (15)

Else Heal
```
**What it Does**
- Marks non-allies entering the area
- Dispels hostile spellcasting
- Punishes hostile attacks with 2d4 Force damage (Strength save)
- Heals allies when no hostile condition is met

**Structure Use**
- If/Than blocks: 3
- And connectors: 6
- Else: 1

**Minimum Vindroth School Level**
- 20
